function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.33!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '6057dddc90e084a129df9cf8073faf984f5565e0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '6057dddc90e084a129df9cf8073faf984f5565e0') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '2a3ce13228fb6ba84cb94273e87d42183590766e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '6057dddc90e084a129df9cf8073faf984f5565e0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('get_description.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: get_description.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('get_description.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): get_description.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('get_description.php') != '8fdb7342458e20e51731b18dcf86a6ab359da7c4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): get_description.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('get_description.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of get_description.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('get_description.php') !== '8fdb7342458e20e51731b18dcf86a6ab359da7c4') {
		if (@sha1_file('get_description.php') !== '767b62ea1d50168feaa555757f09f790bf117968') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: get_description.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('get_description.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('get_description.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('get_description.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('get_description.php') !== '8fdb7342458e20e51731b18dcf86a6ab359da7c4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): get_description.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php') != '02711fe4073cdacf3e813d2cf213e2ea328dec41') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php', 0644)) {

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php') !== '02711fe4073cdacf3e813d2cf213e2ea328dec41') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);

				warn('Creation of backup failed');

		}
